        <script type="text/javascript">
    $LAB.queueWait(
            function () {
                (function (w) {
                    var enabled = true;
                    w.ExpIntentMedia = {
                        reloadIMScript: function () {
                            if (enabled) {
                                if (window.IntentMedia && window.IntentMedia.Event && window.IntentMedia.Event.trigger) {
                                    IntentMedia.Event.trigger('IntentMediaRefresh');
                                } else {
                                    var script = document.createElement('script');
                                    
                                    script.src = 'https://a.cdn.intentmedia.net/javascripts/intent_media_travelocityonexp.js';
                                    document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
                                }
                            }
                        },
                        mergeIMProps: function (propsToMerge) {
                            if (enabled && typeof propsToMerge === 'object') {
                                for (var attrname in propsToMerge) {
                                    if (propsToMerge.hasOwnProperty(attrname) && typeof propsToMerge[attrname] !== 'function') {
                                        if (propsToMerge[attrname].length === 0) {
                                            delete window.IntentMediaProperties[attrname];
                                        } else {
                                            window.IntentMediaProperties[attrname] = propsToMerge[attrname];
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        },
                        fillExitUnit: function () {
                            if (enabled && typeof(window.IntentMedia) === 'object' && typeof(window.IntentMedia.fill_exit_unit) === 'function') {
                                window.IntentMedia.fill_exit_unit();
                            }
                        },
                        pageIdUpdated: function () {
                            if (enabled && typeof(window.IntentMedia) === 'object' && typeof(window.IntentMedia.page_id_updated) === 'function') {
                                window.IntentMedia.page_id_updated();
                            }
                        },
                        isIntentMediaLoaded: function () {
                            return (enabled && typeof(window.IntentMedia) === 'object');
                        }
                    };

                    
                    
                    w.IntentMediaProperties = {};
                    w.IntentMediaProperties.cache_buster = Math.floor(Math.random() * 10000000);
                    w.IntentMediaProperties.screen_width = w.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth || document.body.clientWidth;
                    w.IntentMediaProperties.screen_height = w.innerHeight || document.documentElement.clientHeight || document.body.clientHeight;
                    w.IntentMediaProperties.screen_pixel_depth = w.screen.colorDepth;
                    w.IntentMediaProperties.time_zone_offset = (new Date()).getTimezoneOffset() * -1;
                    w.IntentMediaProperties.display_format_type = document.documentElement.clientWidth > 491 ? "Desktop" : "Mobile";

                })(window);
            }
    );
</script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
    define('alter', function () {
        var alterMap = {};
        var alterMode = 'RELEASED';
        var applicationName = 'car-shopping-web';
        var loggedExperiments = {};

        function msg(nameSpace, key) {
            if (alterMode === 'DEBUG') {
                return '(' + applicationName + ') ' + nameSpace + ': ' + key;
            }

            var alterExperiment = alterMap[nameSpace] && alterMap[nameSpace][key];
            if (alterExperiment) {
                logExperiment(alterExperiment.expResult);
                return alterExperiment.msg;
            }
        }

        function logExperiment(expResult) {
            var id = expResult.experimentId;
            var value = expResult.value;

            if (!loggedExperiments[id]) {
                loggedExperiments[id] = true;

                require('cars.common.analytics', function (analytics) {
                    analytics.logExperiment({ id: id, value: value });
                });
            }
        }

        return {
            msg: msg
        };
    });
</script>
